so those are a couple of the really cool things that romo can do today .	所以 , 這些是romo今天能做的一些很酷的事 。
but i just want to finish by talking about something that we're working on in the future .	但是我只想談談我們在未來所做的事 。
this is actually something that one of our engineers , dom , built in a weekend .	這是我們的工程師 , 一個星期末 , 建造了一個星期末 。
it's built on top of a google open framework called blockly .	它在google開放的架構上 , 叫做 「 街區 」 。
this allows you to drag and drop these blocks of semantic code and create any behavior for this robot you want .	這使你想要 , 讓你想要的 , 讓你想出去 , 讓你想要的行為 , 讓你想要 。
you do not have to know how to code to create a behavior for romo .	你不需要知道如何編碼如何編碼創造出一種行為的行為 。
and you can actually simulate that behavior in the browser , which is what you see romo doing on the left .	你可以模擬在左邊的行為 , 你可以看到romo在左邊做的事 。
and then if you have something you like , you can download it onto your robot and execute it in real life , run the program in real life .	如果你有一些你喜歡的東西 , 你就可以把它下載到你的機器人 , 並在真實生活中進行這個計畫 。
and then if you have something you're proud of , you can share it with every other person who owns a robot in the world .	如果你有了你很驕傲的事 , 你可以分享它 , 和世界上任何人擁有機器人 。
so all of these wifi–enabled robots actually learn from each other .	所以 , 所有這些wifi的機器人可以從彼此學習 。
the reason we're so focused on building robots that everyone can train is that we think the most compelling use cases in personal robotics are personal .	我們非常專注在建造機器人上 , 每個人都可以訓練 , 是因為我們認為最有用的機器人是個人機械人士 。
they change from person to person .	他們從人身上改變 。
so we think that if you're going to have a robot in your home , that robot ought to be a manifestation of your own imagination .	所以我們認為 , 如果你要在你的家裡有一個機器人 , 機器人應該是你自己的想像力 。
so i wish that i could tell you what the future of personal robotics looks like .	所以 , 我希望我能告訴你未來的個人機器人的未來 。
to be honest , i have no idea .	老實說 , 我不知道 。
but what we do know is that it isn't 10 years or 10 billion dollars or a large humanoid robot away .	但我們知道的 , 不是10億美金或10億美金 , 還是一個大型人工機器人 。
the future of personal robotics is happening today , and it's going to depend on small , agile robots like romo and the creativity of people like yourselves .	未來的個人機器人現在正在發生 , 而它將會依賴小型的機器人 , 像是romo和創造力的人 。
so we can't wait to get you all robots , and we can't wait to see what you build .	所以 , 我們不能等待你看到你建造的東西 。
author and activist isabel allende discusses women , creativity , the definition of feminism and , of course , passion in this talk .	作家和活動主義者 , 創作者和活動主義者 , 當然 , 在這個演說中 , 會討論女性主義的定義 。
entertainment , global issues , love , parenting , storytelling , women , world cultures	娛樂 , 全球性議題 , 愛 , 父母 , 故事 , 女人 , 世界文化 。
isabel allende tells tales of passion	伊莎貝爾•阿拉伯爾•所有人都說出了熱情的熱情 。
thank you so much . it's really scary to be here among the smartest of the smart .	謝謝大家 , 非常可怕 , 非常可怕 , 來到這裡的最聰明 。
i'm here to tell you a few tales of passion .	我在這裡要告訴各位一些關於熱情的熱情 。
there's a jewish saying that i love .	有一個猶太人說我愛 。
what is truer than truth ? answer: the story .	什麼比真相更真實 ? 答案:故事 。
i'm a storyteller . i want to convey something that is truer than truth about our common humanity .	我是個故事者 , 我想要傳達出我們常常人類的真相 。
all stories interest me , and some haunt me until i end up writing them .	所有故事都對我有興趣 , 直到我最後寫下這些故事 。
certain themes keep coming up: justice , loyalty , violence , death , political and social issues , freedom .	有些事情會出現:正義、忠誠、暴力、死亡、政治和社會議題、自由 。
i'm aware of the mystery around us , so i write about coincidences , premonitions , emotions , dreams , the power of nature , magic .	我意識到我們周遭的神秘 , 所以我寫了有關巧合、情感、夢想、自然魔法的力量 。
in the last 20 years i have published a few books , but i have lived in anonymity until february of 2006 , when i carried the olympic flag in the winter olympics in italy .	在過去20年 , 我發表了幾本書 , 但在2006年 , 我剛剛出版了幾本書 , 當時我在2006年出版了幾本書 , 直到2006年 , 我在義大利的奧林匹克市旗 。
that made me a celebrity . now people recognize me in macy's , and my grandchildren think that i'm cool .	這使我成為了名人 。 現在人們認出我是酷的 。 現在人們認出我是酷的 。
allow me to tell you about my four minutes of fame .	讓我來告訴你們關於我四分鐘的信息 。
one of the organizers of the olympic ceremony , of the opening ceremony , called me and said that i had been selected to be one of the flagbearers .	奧運會議員之一 , 開放式典禮的其中一位 , 叫我說 , 我被選為是旗幟之一 。
i replied that surely this was a case of mistaken identity because i'm as far as you can get from being an athlete .	我重複這個案例是錯誤的身分 , 因為我身為一個運動員 , 你也可以從運動員身上學到 。
actually , i wasn't even sure that i could go around the stadium without a walker .	實際上 , 我甚至不確定我可以在台上游泳 , 甚至沒有走路 。
i was told that this was no laughing matter .	我被告知這不是笑聲 。
this would be the first time that only women would carry the olympic flag .	這是第一次 , 唯一女性會帶著奧運旗幟 。
five women , representing five continents , and three olympic gold medal winners .	五個大陸 , 還有三個奧林匹克總統 。
my first question was , naturally , what was i going to wear ?	我的第一個問題是 , 天然 , 我會穿什麼 ?
a uniform , she said , and asked for my measurements .	一個制服 , 她說 , 請求我的測量 。
i had a vision of myself in a fluffy anorak , looking like the michelin man .	我在一個充滿感情的景象中 , 看起來像麥可斯曼 。
by the middle of february , i found myself in turin , where enthusiastic crowds cheered when any of the 80 olympic teams was in the street .	在二月時 , 我在街上找到我自己在街上 , 熱烈的群眾歡樂 , 每八十個奧林匹克隊員都在街上 。
those athletes had sacrificed everything to compete in the games .	那些運動員在遊戲中扮演了重要的角色 。
they all deserved to win , but there's the element of luck .	他們都應該要贏 , 但有幸運的運行 。
a speck of snow , an inch of ice , the force of the wind , can determine the result of a race or a game .	一片冰 , 風力的力量 , 風力的力量 , 可以決定結果的結果 , 或比賽的結果 。
however , what matters most more than training or luck is the heart .	然而 , 最重要的訓練或運氣是心臟 。
only a fearless and determined heart will get the gold medal .	只有無懼且堅決的心臟會得到金牌 。
it is all about passion .	而是熱情 。
the streets of turin were covered with red posters announcing the slogan of the olympics .	土耳其的街頭 , 覆蓋著紅色海報 , 宣佈了奧林匹克的街頭 。
passion lives here . isn't it always true ?	熱情生活在這裡 , 不是總是真的嗎 ?
heart is what drives us and determines our fate .	心臟是驅使我們決定我們的命運 。
that is what i need for my characters in my books: a passionate heart .	這就是我在書中所需要的:熱情心臟 。
i need mavericks , dissidents , adventurers , outsiders and rebels , who ask questions , bend the rules and take risks .	我需要mvericks , 不論者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者、外觀者 , 會問問題 , 來改善這些規則 , 並且冒險 。
people like all of you in this room .	像在座的各位一樣 。
nice people with common sense do not make interesting characters .	很有意思的傢伙 , 並不會做出有趣的角色 。
they only make good former spouses .	牠們只能做好的形式 。
in the green room of the stadium , i met the other flag bearers: three athletes , and the actresses susan sarandon and sophia loren .	在綠色房間裡 , 我遇見了其他旗幟:三個運動員 , 和蘇菲亞•洛倫 。
also , two women with passionate hearts: wangari maathai , the nobel prizewinner from kenya who has planted 30 million trees . and by doing so , she has changed the soil , the weather , in some places in africa , and of course the economic conditions in many villages .	另外 , 兩位女士有熱情心臟:wangarimaathai , 來自肯亞的諾貝爾獎得主 , 來自肯亞的諾貝爾獎得主 , 她改變了土壤 , 天氣 , 其他地方 , 在非洲 , 也有許多村落的經濟條件 。
and somaly mam , a cambodian activist who fights passionately against child prostitution .	媽媽 , 一位柬埔寨活動主義者對抗兒童營養機構有很大的影響 。
when she was 14 years old , her grandfather sold her to a brothel .	十四歲時 , 她的祖父把她賣到布魯斯 。
she told us of little girls raped by men who believe that having sex with a very young virgin will cure them from aids .	她告訴我們 , 小女孩被男子強暴 , 那些相信性愛滋病的人會治癒他們愛滋病 。
and of brothels where children are forced to receive five , 15 clients per day , and if they rebel , they are tortured with electricity .	孩子們被迫要接受五個客戶 , 每天有十五個客戶 , 如果他們反叛 , 他們會被強迫接受到五個客戶 。
in the green room i received my uniform .	在綠色房間 , 我接受了我的制服 。
it was not the kind of outfit that i normally wear , but it was far from the michelin man suit that i had anticipated . not bad , really .	這不是我所預期的 。 不錯 , 真的 , 真的很不錯 。
i looked like a refrigerator .	我看起來像是冰箱 。
but so did most of the flagbearers , except sophia loren , the universal symbol of beauty and passion .	但 , 大部分的旗幟都是美麗和熱情的象徵 。
sophia is over 70 and she looks great .	蘇菲亞是70歲 , 她看起來很棒 。
she's sexy , slim and tall , with a deep tan .	她是性愛的 , 高度的 , 用深度的角度來看 。
now , how can you have a deep tan and have no wrinkles ?	現在 , 你要如何有深度的坦尚和沒有皺紋呢 ?
when asked in a tv interview , " how could she look so good ? "	在電視訪問中問: 「 她怎麼能這麼好 ? 」
she replied , " posture . my back is always straight , and i don't make old people's noises . "	她回答: 「 姿勢 , 我不老人的噪音 。 」
so , there you have some free advice from one of the most beautiful women on earth .	所以 , 你有一些自由建議 , 來自世界上最美麗的女性之一 。
no grunting , no coughing , no wheezing , no talking to yourselves , no farting .	沒有發聲 , 沒有開頭 , 沒有打開 , 沒有打開 , 沒有打開 , 沒有打算 。
well , she didn't say that exactly .	嗯 , 她沒有這麼說 。
at some point around midnight , we were summoned to the wings of the stadium , and the loudspeakers announced the olympic flag , and the music started by the way , the same music that starts here , the aida march .	晚上 , 在午夜 , 我們被告知到奧林匹克市旗 , 音樂開始了 , 阿迪達•馬爾斯也開始了 。
sophia loren was right in front of me she's a foot taller than i am , not counting the poofy hair .	蘇菲亞•洛琳在我面前面向我面前 , 她比我還高 , 不算是對的 。
she walked elegantly , like a giraffe on the african savannah , holding the flag on her shoulder . i jogged behind on my tiptoes holding the flag on my extended arm , so that my head was actually under the damn flag .	她很高興地穿著她的肩膀 , 拿著旗幟的旗幟 , 把旗幟放在她的肩膀上 , 把旗幟放在她肩膀上 , 所以我的頭其實是在達姆國旗下 。
all the cameras were , of course , on sophia .	所有的攝影機都在蘇菲亞 。
that was fortunate for me , because in most press photos i appear too , although often between sophia's legs .	這很幸運 , 因為我在索菲亞的雙腿之間 , 很幸運 。
a place where most men would love to be .	在那裡 , 大部分的人會喜歡去的地方 。
the best four minutes of my entire life were those in the olympic stadium .	我整個人生中最好的四分鐘 , 就是在奧林匹克運動場 。
my husband is offended when i say this although i have explained to him that what we do in private usually takes less than four minutes so he shouldn't take it personally .	當我這樣說 , 我跟他說 , 雖然我告訴他 , 我們在私人通常會花不到四分鐘的時間 , 但他不該去做私人的事 。
i have all the press clippings of those four magnificent minutes , because i don't want to forget them when old age destroys my brain cells .	我有這四個美好的動作 , 因為我不想忘記它們 , 老年時 , 我會把它們當老年齡摧毀我的大腦細胞 。
i want to carry in my heart forever the key word of the olympics passion .	我想要帶著我的心靈 , 奧運地帶著 「 奧運 」 的主題 。
so here's a tale of passion .	這是熱情的熱情 。
the year is 1998 , the place is a prison camp for tutsi refugees in congo .	那年是1998年 , 這個地方是一個監獄營營 , 一個囚犯的監獄營 。
by the way , 80 percent of all refugees and displaced people in the world are women and girls .	順帶一提 , 世界上有80%的難民和女性和女孩們 。
we can call this place in congo a death camp , because those who are not killed will die of disease or starvation .	我們可以稱之為 「 死亡營地 」 , 因為那些沒有殺死的人會死亡營 , 因為那些沒有殺死的人會死於疾病或飢餓 。
the protagonists of this story are a young woman , rose mapendo , and her children .	這個故事的主題是一位年輕女子 , 羅斯地圖 , 她的孩子 。
she's pregnant and a widow .	她懷孕了 。
soldiers have forced her to watch as her husband was tortured and killed .	士兵迫使她看著她的丈夫被折磨、殺害 。
somehow she manages to keep her seven children alive , and a few months later , she gives birth to premature twins .	不知如何 , 幾個月後 , 她給出生來養殖雙胞胎 。
two tiny little boys .	兩個小男孩 。
she cuts the umbilical cord with a stick , and ties it with her own hair .	她切割了黏液 , 和她的頭髮結合 。
she names the twins after the camp's commanders to gain their favor , and feeds them with black tea because her milk cannot sustain them .	她的名字叫雙胞胎 , 用黑茶 , 因為她的牛奶無法保持它們 。
when the soldiers burst in her cell to rape her oldest daughter , she grabs hold of her and refuses to let go , even when they hold a gun to her head .	當士兵在她的牢房中傷害 , 她抓住她 , 抓住她 , 抓住她 , 她抓住她抓住她 , 她抓住她抓住她 , 她抓住她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她並拒絕她去 。
somehow , the family survives for 16 months , and then , by extraordinary luck , and the passionate heart of a young american man , sasha chanoff , who manages to put her in a u . s . rescue plane , rose mapendo and her nine children end up in phoenix , arizona , where they're now living and thriving .	不知如何 , 這家生存活了十六個月 , 很不幸地 , 美國人的心臟 , 亞利桑納州 , 亞利桑那州的年輕人 , 他們現在活著和茁壯成長 。
mapendo , in swahili , means great love .	在swahili , 代表偉大的愛 。
the protagonists of my books are strong and passionate women like rose mapendo .	我的書籍的主張是很強烈且熱情的女性 , 比如羅斯•羅斯地圖 。
i don't make them up . there's no need for that .	我不會把它們放出來 , 不需要這樣做 。
i look around and i see them everywhere .	我環繞四周 , 我看到它們 。
i have worked with women and for women all my life .	我和女性和女性一起工作 。
i know them well .	我知道他們很好 。
i was born in ancient times , at the end of the world , in a patriarchal catholic and conservative family .	我出生在古老的時期 , 在世界各地 , 在一個父權主義者和保守家庭 。
no wonder that by age five i was a raging feminist although the term had not reached chile yet , so nobody knew what the heck was wrong with me .	不想五歲時 , 我是一位女權主義者雖然還沒有達到智利 , 所以沒有人知道我是怎麼搞砸的 。
i would soon find out that there was a high price to pay for my freedom , and for questioning the patriarchy .	很快地 , 我很快就會發現 , 有一個高價格要付出我的自由 , 去找尋求助我的自由 。
but i was happy to pay it , because for every blow that i received , i was able to deliver two .	但我很高興能付出它 , 因為每次我收到的每一塊垃圾 , 我都可以傳遞給他們 。
once , when my daughter paula was in her twenties , she said to me that feminism was dated , that i should move on .	一旦 , 當我女兒保羅拉在她的二十歲時 , 她告訴我 , 女性主義是約會的 , 我應該搬進去 。
we had a memorable fight . feminism is dated ?	我們有了不可思議的戰爭 , 女性主義是約會的 ?
yes , for privileged women like my daughter and all of us here today , but not for most of our sisters in the rest of the world who are still forced into premature marriage , prostitution , forced labor they have children that they don't want or they cannot feed .	是的 , 如今我女兒和我們所有人 , 儘管如此 , 大部分的西方世界仍然迫使她們有孩子 , 她們不想要或她們無法餵飽 , 但不希望或無法餵飽 。
they have no control over their bodies or their lives .	他們沒有控制自己的身體或生命 。
they have no education and no freedom .	他們沒有教育 , 也沒有自由 。
they are raped , beaten up and sometimes killed with impunity .	他們被強暴、被逮捕 , 有時被殺害 。
for most western young women of today , being called a feminist is an insult .	現今大部分西方年輕女性主義者是個侮辱 。
feminism has never been sexy , but let me assure you that it never stopped me from flirting , and i have seldom suffered from lack of men .	女性主義從來沒有性感 , 但讓我保證 , 女性主義從來沒有被剝奪 , 我從來沒有性感 , 讓我保證從未被剝奪的女性主義從來沒有性感 。
feminism is not dead , by no means .	女性主義不是死 , 也不是死 。
it has evolved . if you don't like the term , change it , for goddess' sake .	它已經演化了 。 如果你不喜歡這個詞 , 改變它 , 為上帝的命運 。
call it aphrodite , or venus , or bimbo , or whatever you want ; the name doesn't matter , as long as we understand what it is about , and we support it .	稱它為 「 愛 」 、 「 愛 」 、 「 愛 」 、 「 愛 」 、 「 不 」 、 「 不論 」 的名字 , 只要我們了解它是什麼 , 我們就能支持它 。
so here's another tale of passion , and this is a sad one .	這是另一個關於熱情的故事 , 這是個悲傷的例子 。
the place is a small women's clinic in a village in bangladesh .	在孟加拉的一個村落裡 , 一個小女人的診所 。
the year is 2005 .	那是2005年 。
jenny is a young american dental hygienist who has gone to the clinic as a volunteer during her threeweek vacation .	珍妮是一位年輕的美國牙醫師 , 在她三週的牙醫護理時 , 將診所當作志工 。
she's prepared to clean teeth , but when she gets there , she finds out that there are no doctors , no dentists , and the clinic is just a hut full of flies .	她準備乾淨牙齒 , 但當她發現 , 醫生沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 。
outside , there is a line of women who have waited several hours to be treated .	外面 , 有一群婦女在等待幾小時被治療 。
the first patient is in excruciating pain because she has several rotten molars .	第一位患者是很痛苦的 , 因為她有幾個旋轉的動作 。
jenny realizes that the only solution is to pull out the bad teeth .	珍妮意識到 , 唯一的解決方案是要除掉壞牙齒 。
she's not licensed for that ; she has never done it .	她從來沒有做過這種事 , 她從來沒有做過 。
she risks a lot and she's terrified .	她很害怕 。
she doesn't even have the proper instruments , but fortunately she has brought some novocaine .	她甚至沒有適合的儀器 , 但幸運的是她已經帶了一些鼻子 。
jenny has a brave and passionate heart .	珍妮有勇敢和熱情的心 。
she murmurs a prayer and she goes ahead with the operation .	她打開了祈禱 , 帶著禱告 。
at the end , the relieved patient kisses her hands .	最後 , 病人親吻她的手 。
that day the hygienist pulls out many more teeth .	那天 , 衛生棉花了更多牙齒 。
the next morning , when she comes again to the socalled clinic , her first patient is waiting for her with her husband .	隔天早上 , 當她再次到急診室時 , 她的第一個病人在等待她的丈夫 。
the woman's face looks like a watermelon .	女人的臉看起來像是水龍 。
it is so swollen that you can't even see the eyes .	它是很棒的 , 你甚至看不到眼睛 。
the husband , furious , threatens to kill the american .	丈夫 , 威脅要殺死美國人 。
jenny is horrified at what she has done , but then the translator explains that the patient's condition has nothing to do with the operation .	珍妮害怕她做了什麼事 , 但後來翻譯員解釋病人的狀況和手術沒有關係 。
the day before , her husband beat her up because she was not home in time to prepare dinner for him .	隔天之前 , 她丈夫打敗她 , 因為她沒有家去準備晚餐給他 。
millions of women live like this today .	數以百萬計的女性住在今天 。
they are the poorest of the poor .	他們是窮人最窮的人 。
although women do twothirds of the world's labor , they own less than one percent of the world's assets .	儘管女性有三分之二的勞動力 , 但世界各地的勞動力卻不到1% 。
they are paid less than men for the same work if they're paid at all , and they remain vulnerable because they have no economic independence , and they are constantly threatened by exploitation , violence and abuse .	他們的薪水比男性一樣 , 只要他們付出錢 , 他們就會被剝削、暴力、暴力和虐待 。
it is a fact that giving women education , work , the ability to control their own income , inherit and own property , benefits the society .	事實是給予女性教育、工作能力 , 能控制自己的收入、繼承、以及自己的財產 , 能夠控制自己的收入、以及自己的財產 , 讓女性教育 。
if a woman is empowered , her children and her family will be better off .	如果女性有權力 , 她的孩子和家人就會變得更好 。
if families prosper , the village prospers , and eventually so does the whole country .	如果家庭繁榮 , 村落繁殖 , 最終 , 整個國家就會成功 。
wangari maathai goes to a village in kenya .	威利•馬塔哈伊在肯亞的村落 。
she talks with the women and explains that the land is barren because they have cut and sold the trees .	她和婦女談話 , 告訴他們 , 樹木是棕色的 。
she gets the women to plant new trees and water them , drop by drop .	她讓女生植物新的樹木和水 , 以下降落 。
in a matter of five or six years , they have a forest , the soil is enriched , and the village is saved .	在五或六年之內 , 他們有森林 , 土壤被拯救了 。
the poorest and most backward societies are always those that put women down .	最貧窮和最最貧窮最貧窮的社會總是把女性放進去 。
yet this obvious truth is ignored by governments and also by philanthropy .	然而 , 顯然的事實是忽略政府和慈善事業 。
for every dollar given to a women's program , 20 dollars are given to men's programs .	每一塊錢給男性的計畫 , 每一塊錢就有20美元 。
women are 51 percent of humankind .	女性是51%的人 。
empowering them will change everything more than technology and design and entertainment .	賦予他們能改變一切 , 不只是科技、設計和娛樂 。
i can promise you that women working together linked , informed and educated can bring peace and prosperity to this forsaken planet .	我可以保證各位 , 女性一起工作 , 結合在一起 , 受教育 , 能夠讓大家聚集在一起 , 創造和平和繁榮 。
in any war today , most of the casualties are civilians , mainly women and children . they are collateral damage .	在今天的戰爭中 , 大部分的戰爭都是公民 , 主要是女性和孩子 , 主要是女性和孩子 , 主要是女性和孩子 , 主要是女性和孩子 。
men run the world , and look at the mess we have .	男人跑遍世界 , 看看我們所擁有的一切 。
what kind of world do we want ?	我們想要什麼樣的世界 ?
this is a fundamental question that most of us are asking .	這是我們大多數人在問的基本問題 。
does it make sense to participate in the existing world order ?	是否能夠合理參與世界秩序 ?
we want a world where life is preserved and the quality of life is enriched for everybody , not only for the privileged .	我們想要一個世界 , 生活的品質 , 不僅是為了榮幸而生存的品質 。
in january i saw an exhibit of fernando botero's paintings at the uc berkeley library .	在一月 , 我在柏克萊圖書館看到了佛倫多•布萊圖書館的畫作 。
no museum or gallery in the united states , except for the new york gallery that carries botero's work , has dared to show the paintings because the theme is the abu ghraib prison .	在美國 , 沒有博物館或ghraib監獄 , 沒有博物館或ghraib監獄 , 去展示這幅畫 , 因為主題是阿布•巴勒斯博物館 。
they are huge paintings of torture and abuse of power , in the voluminous botero style .	他們是巨大的痛苦和濫用權力 , 在廣闊的波羅風格上 。
i have not been able to get those images out of my mind or my heart .	我沒有辦法把這些影像放在我的腦海或心臟 。
what i fear most is power with impunity .	我害怕大部分的權力是權力 。
i fear abuse of power , and the power to abuse .	我害怕濫用權力 , 而權力被濫用 。
in our species , the alpha males define reality , and force the rest of the pack to accept that reality and follow the rules .	在我們的物種中 , 雄性領袖定義現實 , 並遵守規則 。
the rules change all the time , but they always benefit them , and in this case , the trickledown effect , which does not work in economics , works perfectly .	規則改變了所有時間 , 但他們總是有益處於 , 在這個案例中 , 這種情況下 , 這種情況下 , 這種情況下 , 這種情況下 , 這種情況下 , 最好的效果是 , 在這個案例中 , 這種情況下 ,
abuse trickles down from the top of the ladder to the bottom .	以下降到底層的下層 , 下面是底下的 。
women and children , especially the poor , are at the bottom .	女性和孩子 , 尤其是窮人 , 尤其是窮人 。
even the most destitute of men have someone they can abuse a woman or a child .	即使是最多的女人還是小孩 , 都可以虐待女性或小孩 。
i'm fed up with the power that a few exert over the many through gender , income , race , and class .	我在許多性別、收入、種族和課堂上都有權力 。
i think that the time is ripe to make fundamental changes in our civilization .	我認為 , 時間是用文明來創造基礎的改變 。
but for real change , we need feminine energy in the management of the world .	但真正的改變 , 我們需要女性的能源來管理世界 。
we need a critical number of women in positions of power , and we need to nurture the feminine energy in men .	我們需要針對女性權力的女性權力 , 我們需要培養女性權力的女性 。
i'm talking about men with young minds , of course .	當然 , 我在談的是男性 , 當然 。
old guys are hopeless ; we have to wait for them to die off .	老人是無希望的 。 我們必須等待他們死掉 。
yes , i would love to have sophia loren's long legs and legendary breasts .	是的 , 我很喜歡有蘇菲亞•洛倫長腿和腿部的長腿 。
but given a choice , i would rather have the warrior hearts of wangari maathai , somaly mam , jenny and rose mapendo .	但 , 為了選擇 , 我會有很強烈的戰士 , 瑪莉•瑪麗瑪 , 瑪麗 , 媽媽 , 珍妮 , 和羅斯地圖 。
i want to make this world good .	我想要讓這個世界變得好 。
not better , but to make it good .	不是更好 , 但要讓它好好 。
why not ? it is possible . look around in this room all this knowledge , energy , talent and technology .	為什麼 ? 不行 。 看看這個房間裡的所有知識、能源、科技 。
let's get off our fannies , roll up our sleeves and get to work , passionately , in creating an almost perfect world .	咱們來吃飯 , 熱愛 , 創造一個幾乎完美的世界 。
every day , in a city the size of london , 30 million meals are served . but where does all the food come from ? architect carolyn steel discusses the daily miracle of feeding a city , and shows how ancient food routes shaped the modern world .	每天 , 在城市的大小 , 一座城市的大小 , 一座城市的大小 , 一座城市的大小 , 一座城市的大小 , 一座城市的大小 , 顯示古代的食物如何形成現代世界 。
cities , culture , food , global issues	城市、文化、食物、全球議題 。
carolyn steel: how food shapes our cities	卡羅琳•史黛爾:我們的城市如何塑造我們的城市 。
how do you feed a city ?	你要如何餵飽一個城市 ?
it's one of the great questions of our time .	這是我們時代最棒的問題之一 。
yet it's one that's rarely asked .	但 , 很少人會被問 。
we take it for granted that if we go into a shop or restaurant , or indeed into this theater's foyer in about an hour's time , there is going to be food there waiting for us , having magically come from somewhere .	我們很認真地想 , 只要我們去一間餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 。
but when you think that every day for a city the size of london , enough food has to be produced , transported , bought and sold , cooked , eaten , disposed of , and that something similar has to happen every day for every city on earth , it's remarkable that cities get fed at all .	但當你認為每一天城市都在城市裡 , 運輸、買賣、買賣、買賣、買賣、買賣、煮飯、吃掉 , 不論你想什麼 , 都要被製造出來 , 被運輸、買賣、買賣、買賣、買賣、煮飯、吃掉 , 甚至在地球上發生的一切都很不一樣 。
we live in places like this as if they're the most natural things in the world , forgetting that because we're animals and that we need to eat , we're actually as dependent on the natural world as our ancient ancestors were .	我們生活在這個地方 , 如同我們所居住的環境一樣 , 我們依賴自然世界 , 和我們的古老祖先一樣 。
and as more of us move into cities , more of that natural world is being transformed into extraordinary landscapes like the one behind me it's soybean fields in mato grosso in brazil in order to feed us .	隨著更多人進入城市 , 自然世界已經變成了很棒的地景 , 像是我在巴西的土地景 , 把我們帶進城市裡 , 自然世界已經被轉變成了很棒的景色 。
these are extraordinary landscapes , but few of us ever get to see them .	這些是很不尋常的景觀 , 但少數人看到他們 。
and increasingly these landscapes are not just feeding us either .	越來越多的地景並不只是餵飽我們 。
as more of us move into cities , more of us are eating meat , so that a third of the annual grain crop globally now gets fed to animals rather than to us human animals .	隨著更多人搬進城市裡 , 我們吃肉的數量 , 現今的三分之一的穀物被餵食肉 , 而不是人類的動物 。
and given that it takes three times as much grain actually ten times as much grain to feed a human if it's passed through an animal first , that's not a very efficient way of feeding us .	若有三倍以來餵飽人類 , 這不是很有效率的餵食方式 。
and it's an escalating problem too .	這也是一個嚴重的問題 。
by 2050 , it's estimated that twice the number of us are going to be living in cities .	到2050年 , 估計人口數的人口數量將會住在城市裡 。
and it's also estimated that there is going to be twice as much meat and dairy consumed .	同時也估計有兩倍之多的肉類和dir消耗 。
so meat and urbanism are rising hand in hand .	所以 , 肉和城市主義都在手上 。
and that's going to pose an enormous problem .	這將會造成一個巨大的問題 。
six billion hungry carnivores to feed , by 2050 .	六十億隻飢餓的牛肉 , 到2050年 。
that's a big problem . and actually if we carry on as we are , it's a problem we're very unlikely to be able to solve .	這是個很大的問題 。 事實上如果我們是這樣 , 我們就很不想解決這個問題 。
nineteen million hectares of rainforest are lost every year to create new arable land .	每年有900萬公頃的雨林 , 造成新的可耕地 。
although at the same time we're losing an equivalent amount of existing arables to salinization and erosion .	雖然同樣的時間 , 我們也失去了一種相當大量的存在性 , 可以用來鹽化和消耗 。
we're very hungry for fossil fuels too .	我們對化石燃料也很渴望 。
it takes about 10 calories to produce every calorie of food that we consume in the west .	需要約10卡路里 , 來生產我們消費的食物 。
and even though there is food that we are producing at great cost , we don't actually value it .	儘管我們有食物在大成本的代價上 , 我們並不珍惜它 。
half the food produced in the usa is currently thrown away .	美國有一半的食物被丟棄了 。
and to end all of this , at the end of this long process , we're not even managing to feed the planet properly .	最後 , 在這段漫長的過程中 , 我們還沒辦法餵飽地球 。
a billion of us are obese , while a further billion starve .	我們有十億人是肥胖者 , 而數十億人是肥胖者 。
none of it makes very much sense .	這一點都不太合理 。
and when you think that 80 percent of global trade in food now is controlled by just five multinational corporations , it's a grim picture .	當你認為百分之八十的全球貿易已經被五個跨國公司所控制 , 只是五個跨國公司所控制的 , 這是一張圖片 。
as we're moving into cities , the world is also embracing a western diet .	當我們進入城市時 , 世界也會擁抱西方飲食 。
and if we look to the future , it's an unsustainable diet .	如果我們看看未來 , 它是個不穩定的飲食 。
so how did we get here ?	所以 , 我們是怎麼走到這裡的 ?
and more importantly , what are we going to do about it ?	更重要的是 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
well , to answer the slightly easier question first , about 10 , 000 years ago , i would say , is the beginning of this process in the ancient near east , known as the fertile crescent .	嗯 , 要回答一個更簡單的問題首先 , 大約一萬年前 , 我會說 , 就是這個流程的早期 , 叫做 「 肥沃克里斯 」 。
because , as you can see , it was crescent shaped .	因為 , 如你所見 , 它是有形狀的 。
and it was also fertile .	它也很肥胖 。
and it was here , about 10 , 000 years ago , that two extraordinary inventions , agriculture and urbanism , happened roughly in the same place and at the same time .	大約一萬年前 , 這兩種非凡的發明、農業、農業、城市主義 , 都發生在同一個地方 。
this is no accident , because agriculture and cities are bound together . they need each other .	這不是意外 , 因為農業和城市都聚在一起 , 他們需要彼此 。
because it was discovery of grain by our ancient ancestors for the first time that produced a food source that was large enough and stable enough to support permanent settlements .	因為我們古老的祖先第一次產生出食物來源 , 足以支撐永久的環境 。
and if we look at what those settlements were like , we see they were compact .	如果我們看看這些居住的環境 , 我們看到他們是比較的 。
they were surrounded by productive farm land and dominated by large temple complexes like this one at ur , that were , in fact , effectively , spiritualized , central food distribution centers .	它們被大型的土地覆蓋起來 , 像是這一刻 , 中央食物分配中心食物分配中心的食物分配中心 。
because it was the temples that organized the harvest , gathered in the grain , offered it to the gods , and then offered the grain that the gods didn't eat back to the people .	因為 , 由於穀物所帶來的神殿 , 把穀物取代 , 把穀物給上帝 , 再把穀物給上帝 , 沒吃到上帝 。
so , if you like , the whole spiritual and physical life of these cities was dominated by the grain and the harvest that sustained them .	所以 , 如果你喜歡 , 整個精神和實體生活都是由穀物和穀物所組成的 , 這些城市都是由穀物及收藏所組成的 。
and in fact , that's true of every ancient city .	事實上 , 每個古老的城市都一樣 。
but of course not all of them were that small .	但當然不是所有這些都很小 。
famously , rome had about a million citizens by the first century a . d .	很有名 , 羅馬有大約一百萬個公民 , 羅馬有一百萬個公民 。
so how did a city like this feed itself ?	所以 , 這種城市如何像這樣這樣做 ?
the answer is what i call " ancient food miles . "	答案是 , 我稱之為 「 古代食物哩 」 。
basically , rome had access to the sea , which made it possible for it to import food from a very long way away .	基本上 , 羅馬接近了海洋 , 讓它可以從很長的路徑到海裡 。
this is the only way it was possible to do this in the ancient world , because it was very difficult to transport food over roads , which were rough .	這是在古代世界中唯一的方法 , 因為它很難運送食物 , 路上是很困難的 。
and the food obviously went off very quickly .	食物顯然是很快的 。
so rome effectively waged war on places like carthage and egypt just to get its paws on their grain reserves .	所以羅馬效應的戰鬥 , 像是卡森和埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及他們抓住
and , in fact , you could say that the expansion of the empire was really sort of one long , drawn out militarized shopping spree , really .	事實上 , 你可能會說 , 擴張的擴張是很長的 , 擴張到軍事的擴張 , 真的很長 。
in fact i love the fact , i just have to mention this: rome in fact used to import oysters from london , at one stage . i think that's extraordinary .	事實上 , 我很喜歡這個事實:羅馬其實是來自倫敦的大樓 。 我覺得這是非凡的 。
so rome shaped its hinterland through its appetite .	所以羅馬形塑了它的海底 , 用它的形狀 。
but the interesting thing is that the other thing also happened in the preindustrial world .	但有趣的是 , 另一件事也發生在工業世界 。
if we look at a map of london in the 17th century , we can see that its grain , which is coming in from the thames , along the bottom of this map .	如果我們看看倫敦的地圖的地圖 , 我們可以看到它的地圖是從十七世紀開始的 , 地圖的地圖 。
so the grain markets were to the south of the city .	所以 , 黃金市場就在城市的南方 。
and the roads leading up from them to cheapside , which was the main market , were also grain markets .	從他們到便宜的道路 , 主要市場 , 也是穀物市場 。
and if you look at the name of one of those streets , bread street , you can tell what was going on there 300 years ago .	如果你看看這個名字的名字 , 叫做bread街 , 你可以在300年前就知道了 。
and the same of course was true for fish .	對魚類來說也是如此 。
fish was , of course , coming in by river as well . same thing .	當然 , 魚類也在河流裡 , 也是一樣的 。
and of course billingsgate , famously , was london's fish market , operating onsite here until the mid1980s .	當然 , 很有名的是倫敦的魚市場 , 直到1980年代中期 。
which is extraordinary , really , when you think about it .	這是很不尋常的事 , 當你想到它的時候 。
everybody else was wandering around with mobile phones that looked like bricks and sort of smelly fish happening down on the port .	每個人都穿著手機 , 看起來像是磚塊 , 像磚塊一樣 , 同時也在港口上飛行 。
this is another thing about food in cities: once its roots into the city are established , they very rarely move .	這是另一個關於食物的城市:一旦它根入城市裡 , 它們非常稀少移動 。
meat is a very different story because , of course , animals could walk into the city .	當然 , 動物可以走進城市裡 。
so much of london's meat was coming from the northwest , from scotland and wales .	倫敦的肉來自來自蘇格蘭、蘇格蘭和威爾斯 。
so it was coming in , and arriving at the city at the northwest , which is why smithfield , london's very famous meat market , was located up there .	所以 , 它來到那裡 , 到達北部的冰山 , 這是為什麼smithfield , 倫敦是smithfield , 倫敦非常有名的肉市場 。
poultry was coming in from east anglia and so on , to the northeast .	來自東部的東部 , 到東北方 。
i feel a bit like a weather woman doing this . anyway , and so the birds were coming in with their feet protected with little canvas shoes .	我覺得有點像天氣女性 , 這樣做 , 鳥兒們來到他們腳邊的海岸 , 讓鳥兒來到牠們的腳邊 , 讓鳥兒來到牠們的腳邊 。
and then when they hit the eastern end of cheapside , that's where they were sold , which is why it's called poultry .	接著 , 當他們抵達東方的東方便宜 , 那就被賣出來了 , 這就是為什麼它稱之為 「 大規模 」 。
and , in fact , if you look at the map of any city built before the industrial age , you can trace food coming in to it .	事實上 , 如果你看看在工業時代的地圖 , 你能從產業時代取得食物 。
you can actually see how it was physically shaped by food , both by reading the names of the streets , which give you a lot of clues .	你可以看到它是如何被食物的形狀 , 透過食物 , 透過閱讀街道的名字 , 給你很多線索 。
friday street , in a previous life , is where you went to buy your fish on a friday .	星期五街道 , 在一個星期五的街道上 , 你去買你的魚 。
but also you have to imagine it full of food .	但你必須想像它是充滿食物的 。
because the streets and the public spaces were the only places where food was bought and sold .	因為街道和公共空間只是食物買賣的唯一地方 。
and if we look at an image of smithfield in 1830 you can see that it would have been very difficult to live in a city like this and be unaware of where your food came from .	如果我們看看1930年的圖片 , 你可以看到它會非常困難地住在城市裡 , 像這樣 , 不知你的食物來自哪裡 。
in fact , if you were having sunday lunch , the chances were it was mooing or bleating outside your window about three days earlier .	事實上 , 如果你有星期日的午餐 , 你的機會是在你的窗戶外面 , 或在你的窗戶外面 , 大約三天前 。
so this was obviously an organic city , part of an organic cycle .	這很明顯是有機循環的一部分 。
and then 10 years later everything changed .	接著 , 十年後 , 一切改變了 。
this is an image of the great western in 1840 .	這是1840年大西部的影像 。
and as you can see , some of the earliest train passengers were pigs and sheep .	如你所見 , 最早的訓練乘客是豬和羊 。
so all of a sudden , these animals are no longer walking into market .	突然間 , 這些動物不再走進市場 。
they're being slaughtered out of sight and mind , somewhere in the countryside .	他們被視為是被屠殺 , 不管是在國內的某個地方 。
and they're coming into the city by rail .	然後他們進入城市裡 ,
and this changes everything .	這改變了一切 。
to start off with , it makes it possible for the first time to grow cities , really any size and shape , in any place .	首先 , 要開始發展城市 , 任何地方 , 都可以做得最好 。
cities used to be constrained by geography ; they used to have to get their food through very difficult physical means .	城市以前被地理規劃所限制 , 他們習慣要把食物用在非常困難的物理上 。
all of a sudden they are effectively emancipated from geography .	突然間 , 他們都受到地理學的影響 。
and as you can see from these maps of london , in the 90 years after the trains came , it goes from being a little blob that was quite easy to feed by animals coming in on foot , and so on , to a large splurge , that would be very , very difficult to feed with anybody on foot , either animals or people .	如你所見的 , 在火車之後 , 大約九十年後 , 我們在火車上飛行 , 很容易被動物送到飛機上 , 飛行器是很容易被動物送進去 , 不論是動物或人 , 都很容易餵飽 。
and of course that was just the beginning . after the trains came cars , and really this marks the end of this process .	當然 , 這只是一開始 , 火車結束了 。 火車結束了這個過程 。
it's the final emancipation of the city from any apparent relationship with nature at all .	它是整個城市的最後一個與大自然的聯繫
and this is the kind of city that's devoid of smell , devoid of mess , certainly devoid of people , because nobody would have dreamed of walking in such a landscape .	這是一種城市 , 避免混亂 , 不是因為沒有人會夢想在這樣的地景上 。
in fact , what they did to get food was they got in their cars , drove to a box somewhere on the outskirts , came back with a week's worth of shopping , and wondered what on earth to do with it .	事實上 , 他們的食物是他們買的 , 買了一周的購物 , 買了一週的購物 , 然後想在地球上做些什麼 。
and this really is the moment when our relationship , both with food and cities , changes completely .	這真的是我們的關係 , 食物和城市 , 完全改變了 。
here we have food that used to be the center , the social core of the city at the periphery .	這裡我們有食物被用來成為中心的社會核心 , 城市的核心 。
it used to be a social event , buying and selling food .	以前是社交活動 , 買賣食物 。
we used to cook ; now we just add water , or a little bit of an egg if you're making a cake or something .	我們以前會煮飯 , 只是加入水 , 或一些蛋糕 , 或一些蛋糕 。
we don't smell food to see if it's okay to eat .	我們不會聞到食物 , 看看它是否好吃 。
we just read the back of a label on a packet .	我們只是在一個標籤貼上標記 。
and we don't value food . we don't trust it .	而我們不珍惜食物 , 我們不相信它 。
so instead of trusting it , we fear it .	所以 , 我們不相信它 , 我們害怕它 。
and instead of valuing it , we throw it away .	而不是評估它 , 我們把它丟掉 。
one of the great ironies of modern food systems is that they've made the very thing they promised to make easier much harder .	現代食物系統的最大諷刺之一就是他們做了一件很棒的諷刺 , 就是他們製造了很大的諷刺 。
by making it possible to build cities anywhere and any place , they've actually distanced us from our most important relationship , which is that of us and nature .	藉由創造城市 , 任何地方 , 都可以在任何地方建立城市 , 不論是我們和大自然 。
and also they've made us dependent on systems that only they can deliver , that , as we've seen , are unsustainable .	而且他們也讓我們依賴系統 , 只能提供我們所看到的 , 不穩定 。
so what are we going to do about that ?	所以 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
it's not a new question .	這不是一個新的問題 。
500 years ago it's what thomas more was asking himself .	五百年前 , 湯瑪斯會問自己 。
this is the frontispiece of his book " utopia . "	這是他的書《烏托邦》 。
and it was a series of semiindependent citystates , if that sounds remotely familiar , a day's walk from one another where everyone was basically farmingmad , and grew vegetables in their back gardens , and ate communal meals together , and so on .	它是一系列獨立的餐廳 , 如果聽起來很熟悉 , 每人都很熟悉 , 每一間餐廳都很熟悉 , 日常生活在後菜園裡 , 再生長蔬菜 , 再加上餐具 , 再加上餐具 。
and i think you could argue that food is a fundamental ordering principle of utopia , even though more never framed it that way .	我想你可以說食物是烏托邦的基本原則 , 儘管從來不是如此 。
and here is another very famous " utopian " vision , that of ebenezer howard , " the garden city . "	這裡還有另一個非常著名的烏托邦 「 烏托邦 」 的景象 , 叫做烏托邦的 「 烏托邦 」 。
same idea: series of semiindependent citystates , little blobs of metropolitan stuff with arable land around , joined to one another by railway .	同樣的點子:一系列獨立的城市 , 單獨的城市 , 一大堆的獨立城市 , 加入了一輛獨立的城市 。
and again , food could be said to be the ordering principle of his vision .	再次 , 食物可以被說是他的視野的原理 。
it even got built , but nothing to do with this vision that howard had .	它甚至建造了 , 但沒有用這個視覺去做 。
and that is the problem with these utopian ideas , that they are utopian .	這些烏托邦的問題是烏托邦 。
utopia was actually a word that thomas moore used deliberately .	烏托邦實際上是湯瑪斯•摩爾使用的詞 。
it was a kind of joke , because it's got a double derivation from the greek .	這是個笑話 , 因為它有來自希臘的高峰 。
it can either mean a good place , or no place .	它可以代表一個好地方 , 或沒有地方 。
because it's an ideal . it's an imaginary thing . we can't have it .	因為這是一個理想 , 一個不可思議的理想 , 我們無法做到 。
and i think , as a conceptual tool for thinking about the very deep problem of human dwelling , that makes it not much use .	我認為 , 作為一個概念性的工具 , 來思考人類的深度問題 , 會讓它不用 。
so i've come up with an alternative , which is sitopia , from the ancient greek , " sitos " for food , and " topos " for place .	所以 , 我得到了另一個替代方案 , 例如: 「 stopia 」 , 來自古希臘、 「 stopia 」 、 「 stopia 」 、 「 stopia 」 。
i believe we already live in sitopia .	我相信我們已經住在烏托邦 。
we live in a world shaped by food , and if we realize that , we can use food as a really powerful tool a conceptual tool , design tool , to shape the world differently .	我們生活在世界各地 , 如同我們所知的工具 , 設計工具 , 設計工具 , 來塑造世界不同 。
so if we were to do that , what might sitopia look like ?	所以如果我們這樣做 , 西雅圖像什麼樣子 ?
well i think it looks a bit like this .	我覺得它看起來有點像這樣 。
i have to use this slide . it's just the look on the face of the dog .	我必須用這張投影片 , 只是在狗的臉上 。
but anyway , this is it's food at the center of life , at the center of family life , being celebrated , being enjoyed , people taking time for it .	不管怎樣 , 這是食物在生活的中心 , 家庭生活的中心 , 家庭生活的中心 , 被慶祝 , 享受 , 人們花時間 。
this is where food should be in our society .	食物應該在我們的社會裡 。
but you can't have scenes like this unless you have people like this .	但你不能像這樣 , 除非你有這樣的人 。
by the way , these can be men as well .	順帶一提 , 這些都是男性 。
it's people who think about food , who think ahead , who plan , who can stare at a pile of raw vegetables and actually recognize them .	人們會想到食物 , 想到食物 , 誰會想到食物 , 想到食物 , 誰會想到食物 , 誰會想到食物 , 誰會想到食物呢 ?
we need these people . we're part of a network .	我們需要這些人 , 我們是網路的一部分 。
because without these kinds of people we can't have places like this .	因為如果沒有這些人 , 我們就不能像這樣 。
here , i deliberately chose this because it is a man buying a vegetable .	在這裡 , 我真的選擇了因為它是個男人買蔬菜 。
but networks , markets where food is being grown locally .	但網路 , 市場 , 食物正在成長的地方 。
it's common . it's fresh .	它很常見 , 很常見 。
it's part of the social life of the city .	它是社會生活的一部分 。
because without that , you can't have this kind of place , food that is grown locally and also is part of the landscape , and is not just a zerosum commodity off in some unseen hellhole .	因為 , 沒有這種地方 , 你不能有這種地方 , 食物也就是地景的一部分 , 而不是僅僅是地景的一部分 , 而不是只是一個零和零的產物 。
cows with a view .	牛 , 用一個觀點 。
steaming piles of humus .	蒸發的熱帶 。
this is basically bringing the whole thing together .	這基本上就是把整合在一起 。
and this is a community project i visited recently in toronto .	這是我最近參加的社區專案計畫 。
it's a greenhouse , where kids get told all about food and growing their own food .	這是溫室 , 孩子們都被告知食物和種植的食物 。
here is a plant called kevin , or maybe it's a plant belonging to a kid called kevin . i don't know .	這裡有一個叫做kevin的植物 , 或者它是植物屬於一個叫做kevin的孩子 , 或許它是個植物 , 叫做凱文 。 我不知道 。
but anyway , these kinds of projects that are trying to reconnect us with nature is extremely important .	總之 , 這些計畫正在嘗試與大自然的關聯性非常重要 。
so sitopia , for me , is really a way of seeing .	所以 , 西托比亞 , 對我來說 , 這是一種看待方式 。
it's basically recognizing that sitopia already exists in little pockets everywhere .	基本上 , 在小小的口袋裡 , 每個角落都有一些口袋 。
the trick is to join them up , to use food as a way of seeing .	技巧是要加入它們 , 用食物作為一種看待方式 。
and if we do that , we're going to stop seeing cities as big , metropolitan , unproductive blobs , like this .	如果我們這樣做 , 我們會停止看到城市 , 像這樣 , 大型、不生產力的城市 , 像這樣 。
we're going to see them more like this , as part of the productive , organic framework of which they are inevitably a part , symbiotically connected .	我們會看到它們是有機架構的 , 有機架構 , 不可避免地 , 有機架構造 , 其中一部分是有機架構 , 無可避免地連結 。
but of course , that's not a great image either , because we need not to be producing food like this anymore .	當然 , 這不是很棒的圖像 , 因為我們需要不要再生產食物 。
we need to be thinking more about permaculture , which is why i think this image just sums up for me the kind of thinking we need to be doing .	我們需要思考更多關於農業的思維 , 這就是為什麼我認為這張圖像剛剛提到我們要做的事 。
it's a reconceptualization of the way food shapes our lives .	它是一種重新概念化的食物塑造我們的生活方式 。
the best image i know of this is from 650 years ago .	最好的圖像是我從650年前拍攝的 。
it's ambrogio lorenzetti's " allegory of good government . "	這是亞伯羅•洛倫澤蒂的 「 政府的優秀政府 」 。
it's about the relationship between the city and the countryside .	它是關於城市和國家之間的關係 。
and i think the message of this is very clear .	我認為這個訊息非常清楚 。
if the city looks after the country , the country will look after the city .	如果城市在城市看 , 國家就會看到這個城市 。
and i want us to ask now , what would ambrogio lorenzetti paint if he painted this image today ?	今天我想我們來問 , 如果他畫畫這張圖像現在 , 阿布羅•洛倫澤蒂畫畫呢 ?
what would an allegory of good government look like today ?	現今 , 政府的政策是怎樣的 ?
because i think it's an urgent question .	因為我認為這是一個迫切的問題 。
it's one we have to ask , and we have to start answering .	這是我們必須開始回答的 。
we know we are what we eat .	我們知道我們是吃的 。
we need to realize that the world is also what we eat .	我們必須意識到 , 世界也是我們吃的 。
but if we take that idea , we can use food as a really powerful tool to shape the world better .	但如果我們採取這個想法 , 我們就能用食物來塑造世界更好的工具 。
weeks from the charter for compassion launch , karen armstrong looks at religion's role in the 21st century: will its dogmas divide us ? or will it unite us for common good ? she reviews the catalysts that can drive the world's faiths to rediscover the golden rule .	從慈悲的一週 , 卡爾•阿姆斯壯觀看宗教的角色 , 在21世紀 , 說: 「 把黃金法案放到哪裡去 ? 」 還是會讓世界的信仰轉變為 「 同理心 」 , 克拉斯•阿姆斯壯觀看宗教的角色在21世紀:它會把黃金法案放到哪裡 ?
god , ted prize , global issues , politics , religion , tedglobal2009 , violence	上帝 , ted , 全球議題 , 政治 , 宗教 , tedprize , 全球議題 , 政治 , 宗教 , tedprize , 全球議題 。
karen armstrong: let's revive the golden rule	karenmstrong:讓我們重新保證黃金法則 。
for years i've been feeling frustrated , because as a religious historian , i've become acutely aware of the centrality of compassion in all the major world faiths .	多年來 , 我變得很沮喪 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我變得很沮喪 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我已經變得很沮喪 , 因為身為一位宗教歷史學家 , 我已經變得很沮喪 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我一直感到挫折 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我已經變得很沮喪 。
every single one of them has evolved their own version of what's been called the golden rule .	每一個人都演化出自己的版本 , 叫做黃金法則 。
sometimes it comes in a positive version " always treat all others as you'd like to be treated yourself . "	有時候它會出現在正面的版本中: 「 總是對待你自己的人 。 」
and equally important is the negative version " don't do to others what you would not like them to do to you . "	同樣重要的是負面版本: 「 別對其他人做你不喜歡他們做的事 。 」
look into your own heart , discover what it is that gives you pain and then refuse , under any circumstance whatsoever , to inflict that pain on anybody else .	看看你自己的心臟 , 發現它是什麼 , 讓你痛苦 , 然後拒絕 , 在任何情況下 , 在任何情況下 , 都會造成疼痛 。
and people have emphasized the importance of compassion , not just because it sounds good , but because it works .	人們強調了同情心的重要性 , 不只是因為它聽起來很好 , 而是因為它運作得很好 。
people have found that when they have implemented the golden rule as confucius said , " all day and every day , " not just a question of doing your good deed for the day and then returning to a life of greed and egotism , but to do it all day and every day , you dethrone yourself from the center of your world , put another there , and you transcend yourself .	人們發現 , 當他們把黃金法規定為 「 白天 」 時 , 每天都跟你說: 「 所有日子 , 不只在你人生中 , 去做你的好事 , 然後再回到人生中 , 成長和生態 , 直到你在世界各地走進去 , 再次走向你自己 , 再來到你的生活中 , 再次走向你自己 。
and it brings you into the presence of what's been called god , nirvana , rama , tao .	它將你帶到一個被稱為神、公共、國內、公共場所的所謂上帝 。
something that goes beyond what we know in our egobound existence .	在我們所知的事物中 , 發生了什麼事 。
but you know you'd never know it a lot of the time , that this was so central to the religious life .	但你知道你永遠不會知道太多時間 , 這是宗教生活的中心 。
because with a few wonderful exceptions , very often when religious people come together , religious leaders come together , they're arguing about abstruse doctrines or uttering a council of hatred or inveighing against homosexuality or something of that sort .	因為有一些很棒的例外 , 通常當宗教領袖聚在一起時 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 他們會爭論 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖團聚在一起 , 宗教領袖聚在一起 , 他們爭論
often people don't really want to be compassionate .	通常人們並不想同情心 。
i sometimes see when i'm speaking to a congregation of religious people a sort of mutinous expression crossing their faces because people often want to be right instead .	我有時候會看到當我說到宗教人的表情時 , 會被視為是對的 , 反而是對的 。
and that of course defeats the object of the exercise .	這當然是運動的目標 。
now why was i so grateful to ted ?	為什麼我這麼感謝ted ?
because they took me very gently from my booklined study and brought me into the 21st century , enabling me to speak to a much , much wider audience than i could have ever conceived .	因為他們把我帶到21世紀 , 把我帶到一個更廣大的廣場上 , 讓我能從我的書線研究中帶領我 , 把我帶到一個更廣闊的觀眾 。
because i feel an urgency about this .	因為我覺得很急迫 。
if we don't manage to implement the golden rule globally , so that we treat all peoples , wherever and whoever they may be , as though they were as important as ourselves , i doubt that we'll have a viable world to hand on to the next generation .	如果我們不用統治全球的方式 , 以便我們對待所有人 , 無論是誰 , 無論如何 , 他們都很重要 , 我懷疑我們有能力可以在下一代代代 。
the task of our time , one of the great tasks of our time , is to build a global society , as i said , where people can live together in peace .	我們的工作任務之一 , 就是建立一個全球社會 , 如我所說 , 人們可以一起生活和平 。
and the religions that should be making a major contribution are instead seen as part of the problem .	而宗教應該要做出主要貢獻 , 而不是被視為是問題的一部分 。
and of course it's not just religious people who believe in the golden rule .	當然 , 這不僅僅是宗教相信黃金法則的人 。
this is the source of all morality , this imaginative act of empathy , putting yourself in the place of another .	這是所有道德的源頭 , 同理心 , 同理心 , 把自己放到另一個地方 。
and so we have a choice , it seems to me .	所以 , 我們有選擇 , 似乎是我 。
we can either go on bringing out or emphasizing the dogmatic and intolerant aspects of our faith , or we can go back to the rabbis . rabbi hillel , the older contemporary of jesus , who , when asked by a pagan to sum up the whole of jewish teaching while he stood on one leg , said , " that which is hateful to you , do not do to your neighbor .	可以說: 「 這對你的鄰居有多大的貢獻 , 不管你在哪裡 , 不管你在哪裡 , 都不對你的鄰居說話 。 」 說: 「 這對你來說是很討厭的 , 對你來說 , 這對你的鄰居是不對的 。
that is the torah and everything else is only commentary . "	重點是 , 所有其他只是評論 。 」
and the rabbis and the early fathers of the church who said that any interpretation of scripture that bred hatred and disdain was illegitimate .	拉比和早期的父親 , 教堂的說法 , 教會說任何詮釋的可能性 , 都是違法的 。
and we need to revive that spirit .	我們需要重新維持精神 。
and it's not just going to happen because a spirit of love wafts us down .	這並不會發生 , 因為靈感的靈感會讓我們下下 。
we have to make this happen , and we can do it with the modern communications that ted has introduced .	我們必須這樣做 , 我們也能用現代的溝通方式來做這件事 。

in singapore , we have a group going to use the charter to heal divisions recently that have sprung up in singaporean society , and some members of the parliament want to implement it politically .	在新加坡 , 我們有一群人在新加坡的新加坡上 , 有些成員會在新加坡社群中採取行動 , 其中一些成員會想實現它的政治 。

religious teaching , this is where we've gone so wrong , concentrating solely on believing abstruse doctrines .	宗教教學 , 這是我們走出錯的地方 , 聚焦在信仰的教學上 。
religious teaching must always lead to action .	宗教教學必須總是引領行動 。

and i want to continue with our partners to do two things educate and stimulate compassionate thinking .	我希望繼續與我們的合作夥伴一起做兩件事 , 教育和激勵人心思維 。

people often think it simply means feeling sorry for somebody .	人們通常覺得對某人來說 , 感覺很抱歉 。

the same applies to educators .	同樣的應用程式給教育者 。
i'd like youth to get a sense of the dynamism , the dynamic and challenge of a compassionate lifestyle .	我希望你們能感受到動態和挑戰 , 一個充滿同情心的生活方式的動態和挑戰 。

and i am convinced .	我很相信 。

" pigeon's progress " struck me as a catchy title .	「 鴿子的進步 」 帶著我身為一隻貓頭鷹 。

so it's a homeless pigeon now and it's going to have to find another place to live , and that allows me to go through my catalog of favorite things , and we start with the tall ones and so on .	所以這是一個無家可歸的旅程 , 在那裡 , 我必須找到另一個地方 , 這樣我才能找到另一個地方 , 在那裡 , 我得找到另一個地方 , 這樣我就可以從高度的角度開始 。

through the alley , we can see the impact is captured in the red line .	透過這條線 , 我們可以看到衝擊在紅線中被捕捉 。

we get a little exuberant as we pass gesu ; it's not surprising to sort of mimic the architecture in this way .	當我們通過gesu時 , 它並不驚奇 , 要模仿這個建築物 。

as we look at the drawing board , we see what he's working on is , in fact , a map of the journey that the pigeon has just taken , and the red line extends through all the sights .	當我們看著畫板時 , 我們看到他正在做的事情 , 紅線延伸到所有洞穴的地圖 。
